1b1(rgyud 'bum): rgya gar skad du/ Ar+ya pany+tsa bing sha ti pradz+nyA pA ra mi tA mu kha nA ma ma hA yA na
1b2(rgyud 'bum): sU tra/ bod skad du/ 'phags pa shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa sgo nyi shu rtsa lnga pa zhes bya ba
1b3(rgyud 'bum): theg pa chen po'i mdo/ sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la phyag 'tshal
2a1(rgyud 'bum): lo// 'di skad bdag gis thos pa dus gcig na/ bcom ldan 'das ri rab kyi choms
2a2(rgyud 'bum): la lha thams cad kyi mtshan mo'i gnas na/ byang chub sems dpa' bye ba khrag khrig 'bum phrag du ma
2a3(rgyud 'bum): dang thabs cig tu bzhugs te/ de nas bcom ldan 'das lha dang / lha'i bu dang / lha ma yin dang /
2a4(rgyud 'bum): rlung lA dang / nam mkha' lding dang / klu dang / gnod sprin dang / mi 'am ci dang / srin po dang /
2b1(rgyud 'bum): rig sngags 'chang thams cad dang / 'byung po dang / log 'dren dang / sha za dang / snang ba dang / mi snang ba'i ma
2b2(rgyud 'bum): mo'i tshogs shin tu mang zhing rgya che ba dpag tshad lnga'i dkyil 'khor du 'dus pa sha stag dang / dge slong stong nyis brgya lnga/
2b3(rgyud 'bum): bcus bskor cing mdun du bdar nas chos ston te/ de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po lag na rdo rje//
2b4(rgyud 'bum): rdo rje'i rigs thams cad kyis yongs su bskor cing rig pa'i tshogs dang / phyag rgya'i tshogs de dag thams cad kyi
2b5(rgyud 'bum): rig sngags 'chang bye ba phrag du mas yongs su bskor nas/ bcom ldan 'das ga la ba der song ste phyin nas par
3a1(rgyud 'bum): snang las babs nas/ bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs la mgo bos phyag 'tshal te/ bcom ldan 'das
3a2(rgyud 'bum): la lan gsum bskor ba byas nas phyogs gcig tu 'dug pa dang / de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis/ gsang ba'i bdag po lag
3a3(rgyud 'bum): nA rdo rje la bka' stsal pa/ gsang ba'i bdag po nyi shu rtsa lnga po 'di rnams ni/ nga'i shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo yin no//
3a4(rgyud 'bum): oM sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la phyag 'tshal lo// oM byang chub kyi sems rdo rje shes rab kyi pha rol tu
3a5(rgyud 'bum): phyin pa'i sgo'o/ / oM kun tu bzang po spyod pa shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM yid bzhin gyi nor bu shes rab kyi
3a6(rgyud 'bum): pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o/ / oM 'gog pa med pa shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM skye bar 'gyur ba shes rab kyi pha
3b1(rgyud 'bum): rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o/ / oM rnam par shes pa thams cad shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM 'bar ba chen po'i chos nyid shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM brtson
3b2(rgyud 'bum): 'grus shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o/ / oM thams cad du 'gro ba shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM rdo rje thams cad brtan pa'i sems shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o//
3b3(rgyud 'bum): oM de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM rang bzhin rnam par dag pa'i chos nyid ye shes rnam par dag pa shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM
3b4(rgyud 'bum): las rnam par sbyong ba shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o/ / oM nges par gnod mdzes rdo rje can phaT shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM 'dod pa la 'dod chags rnam par dag pa shes
3b5(rgyud 'bum): rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o/ / oM mgyogs pa'i rdo rje can shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM hUM thams cad du 'gro ba shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM hriHshes rab kyi pha
3b6(rgyud 'bum): rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o/ / oM a zhes bya ba'i sgo shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM aM ba hUM shes rab kyi pha rol tu
3b7(rgyud 'bum): phyin pa'i sgo'o/ / oM oM shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku'i mchog shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// oM de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad
4a1(rgyud 'bum): kyi gsung rnam par dag pa shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o/ / oM de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi thugs kyi rdo rje shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo'o// bcom
4a2(rgyud 'bum): ldan 'das kyis de skad ces bka' stsal nas/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po lag na rdo rje dang / thams cad dang ldan pa'i 'khor de dang / lha dang / mi dang / lha ma yin dang /
4a3(rgyud 'bum): dri zar bcas pa'i 'jig rten yi rangs te/ bcom ldan 'das kyis gsungs pa la mngon par bstod do// 'phags pa shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo nyi shu rtsa lnga pa zhes bya ba theg pa chen
4a4(rgyud 'bum): po'i mdo rdzogs so/ / / @rgya gar skad du/ sarba ta thA ga ta kA ya bA k+Shit+ta gu h+ya a lad+hA ra byA ho tan+na rA dza nA ma/ bod skad du/ de bzhin gshegs pa
4a5(rgyud 'bum): thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs kyi gsang ba rgyan gyi bkod pa zhes bya ba'i rgyud kyi rgyal po/ bla ma dang 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi zhabs kyi pad+mo la gus par phyag 'tshal lo// 'di skad
4a6(rgyud 'bum): bdag gis thos pa dus gcig na/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje ye shes rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug chen po dang / de bzhin gshegs
4a7(rgyud 'bum): pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje ye shes phyag rgya chen po'i dam tshig gi byin gyi rlabs kyi rdo rje'i sku chen po dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs
4b1(rgyud 'bum): rdo rje ye shes rin po che chen po'i cod pan gyi rtse mo'i gtsug phud kyis dbang bskur ba brnyes pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje ye shes kyi ting nge
4b2(rgyud 'bum): 'dzin chen po dang ldan pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje ye shes kyi las sna tshogs pa chen po dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku
4b3(rgyud 'bum): dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje ye shes mchod pa chen po spro ba'i dam tshig gi gsang ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje ye shes dkyil 'khor
4b4(rgyud 'bum): chen po dam tshig gi de kho na nyid dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje ye shes gsang ba chen po'i snying po dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku
4b5(rgyud 'bum): dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje ye shes kyi mnga' bdag chen po dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje ye shes kun tu bzang po dang / de bzhin
4b6(rgyud 'bum): gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje ye shes dpe med cing mi mnyam pa dang mnyam pa nam mkha' lta bu dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung
4b7(rgyud 'bum): dang / thugs rdo rje rigs dang / snying po dang / phyag rgya dang / gsang sngags dang / rig pa gnyis su med par gyur pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang /
5a1(rgyud 'bum): thugs rdo rje ye shes pha rol tu phyin pa'i snying po la dga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje ye shes kyi lhag pa'i lha'i snying
5a2(rgyud 'bum): po mdzes pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje ye shes rgyan chen po bkod pa'i dkyil 'khor chen po'i snying po la/ nam mkha'i khams thams cad kyi
5a3(rgyud 'bum): rdul phra rab kyi rdul dang mnyam pa'i rdo rje ye shes chen po 'ba' zhig dang thabs cig tu bzhugs so/ / de'ang 'di lta ste/ sgo mtha' yas pa zhes bya ba'i rdo rje yum chen mo dang / nam mkha'i sgo zhes
5a4(rgyud 'bum): bya ba'i rdo rje yum chen mo dang / a po dza'i sgo zhes bya ba'i rdo rje yum chen mo dang / 'gyur ba med pa'i sgo zhes bya ba'i rdo rje yum chen mo dang / shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin ma zhes bya ba'i rdo rje yum
5a5(rgyud 'bum): chen mo dang / gzhan yang ma lus shing lus pa med pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rdul phra rab dang mnyam pa'i brtson 'grus dang ldan pa'i rdo rje btsun mo stong phrag brgya la'ang 'di lta ste/ mda'i mtshon
5a6(rgyud 'bum): cha'i lag ces bya ba'i rdo rje btsun mo dang / dbang phyug la lta ba'i rim pa zhes bya ba'i rdo rje btsun mo dang / nye bar zhi ba'i bzhin ras zhes bya ba'i rdo rje btsun mo dang / rkyen du lta ba'i bzhin ras
5a7(rgyud 'bum): zhes bya ba'i rdo rje btsun mo dang / 'dod pa'i zla mtshan rdo rje zhes bya ba'i rdo rje btsun mo dang / brda sprod pa ma zhes bya ba'i rdo rje btsun mo dang / 'bri ba'i sgo zhes bya ba'i rdo rje btsun mo dang / rol pa
5b1(rgyud 'bum): dang ldan pa zhes bya ba'i rdo rje btsun mo dang / 'dod pa'i mchog ces bya ba'i rdo rje btsun mo dang / dbang phyug gis bde ba'i sgo zhes bya ba'i rdo rje btsun mo dang / dmigs pa'i sgo zhes bya ba'i rdo rje btsun
5b2(rgyud 'bum): mo dang / brang las skyes zhes bya ba'i rdo rje btsun mo ste/ de dag la sogs pa rdo rje btsun mo rnams kyis yongs su bskor cing mdun du bdar to// gzhan yang dpag tu med pa'i rdo rje pho nya ma chen mo rnams
5b3(rgyud 'bum): dang thabs cig tu bzhugs te/ de'ang 'di lta ste/ snying skul bar byed pa zhes bya ba'i rdo rje pho nya mo chen mo dang / gdug pa thams cad 'gugs pa zhes bya ba'i rdo rje pho nya mo chen mo dang / rjes su mnyes
5b4(rgyud 'bum): pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i rdo rje pho nya mo chen mo dang / khrag 'gugs pa zhes bya ba'i rdo rje pho nya mo chen mo dang / thams cad 'phrog pa zhes bya ba'i rdo rje pho nya mo chen mo la sogs pa'o// gzhan yang 'jig rten
5b5(rgyud 'bum): gyi khams rgyas pa'i rdo rje sgo srungs ma chen mo rnams dang yang thabs cig ste/ de'ang 'di lta ste/ rdo rje 'bebs pa zhes bya ba'i rdo rje sgo srungs ma chen mo dang / dam tshig gsum ldan zhes bya ba'i rdo rje sgo
5b6(rgyud 'bum): srungs ma chen mo dang / 'jig pa'i yan lag can zhes bya ba'i rdo rje sgo srungs ma chen mo dang / thog ma pa zhes bya ba'i rdo rje sgo srungs ma chen mo dang / gdul dka' 'dul zhes bya ba'i rdo rje sgo srungs ma
5b7(rgyud 'bum): chen mo la sogs pa'o/ / gzhan yang mi mnyam pa dang mnyam pa'i rdo rje bran mo chen mo rnams dang yang thabs cig ste/ de'ang 'di lta ste/ sku gsung thugs thams cad rdo rjes 'ching ba ma zhes bya ba'i
6a1(rgyud 'bum): rdo rje bran mo chen mo dang / 'jigs pa'i me'i gdong zhes bya ba'i rdo rje bran mo chen mo dang / gtsigs shing rnam par 'gyur ba'i gdong zhes bya ba'i rdo rje bran mo chen mo dang / 'jig
6a2(rgyud 'bum): rten gsum 'ching ba zhes bya ba'i rdo rje bran mo chen mo dang / bskal par gnas pa zhes bya ba la sogs pa'i rdo rje bran mo chen mo'o// gzhan yang dpe med pa'i rdo rje rol pa mo chen mo rnams dang yang
6a3(rgyud 'bum): thabs cig ste/ de'ang 'di lta ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku gsung thugs rdo rje dgyes pa zhes bya ba'i rdo rje rol pa chen mo dang / kun nas 'bebs pa zhes bya ba'i rdo rje rol pa chen mo
6a4(rgyud 'bum): dang / 'jig rten gsum rab tu 'joms pa zhes bya ba'i rdo rje rol pa chen mo dang / rab tu dga' ba'i rjes su 'gro ba zhes bya ba'i rdo rje rol pa chen mo dang / thams cad dga' bar byed pa zhes bya ba'i
6a5(rgyud 'bum): rdo rje rol pa chen mo la sogs pa'o/ / gzhan yang nam mkha'i khams thams cad rgyas par gang ba'i rdo rje'i yab rnams dang yang thabs cig ste/ de'ang 'di lta ste/ 'dod pa'i dbang phyug ces bya
6a6(rgyud 'bum): ba'i rdo rje yab chen po dang / mkha' 'gro'i rdo rje dbang phyug dang / dri yi dbang phyug dang / stug po bkod pa dang / zla ba'i 'od dang / 'dun pa bsrel dang / skye bo yongs su dor ba dang / legs par
6a7(rgyud 'bum): sbyangs pa dang / 'dod pa'i rdo rje dang / gdung ba skyed pa dang / 'dul bar byed pa dang / gdug pa thams cad sel bar byed pa dang / de kho na nyid kyi mgon po dang / gnas pa po dang / brtse ba can dang /
6b1(rgyud 'bum): chos 'chang dang / bskyod pa po dang / spro ba po dang / 'ching ba po dang / skor ba po dang / de dag la sogs pa rdo rje yab rnams so// gzhan yang mtha' yas pa'i rdo rje pho nya mo 'phrog pa'i rdo rje
6b2(rgyud 'bum): bran po rdo rje'i tshogs dang thabs cig ste/ de'ang 'di lta ste/ rdo rje rlung zhes bya ba dang / rdo rje me dang / rdo rje mi 'khrugs pa dang / rdo rje chu dang / gzhan yang rdo rje rgyal po chen po bzhi la/ 'di
6b3(rgyud 'bum): lta ste/ zhi bar byed pa dang / rgyas par byed pa dang / dbang du byed pa dang / mi shes pa thams cad zad par byed pa ste/ de dag la sogs pa'o// gzhan yang mchog tu rgya chen po sangs rgyas kyi
6b4(rgyud 'bum): ye shes rab tu gnas pa'i mchod pa dang ldan pa bcom ldan 'das ston pa rtag pa mchog gi mnga' bdag ste/ kun tu bzang po'i sku yis ni// 'jig rten gsum gyi dkyil 'khor spros// bcom
6b5(rgyud 'bum): ldan rdo rje 'dzin legs bzhugs/ / gsang ba rgyan gyi sbyor bas so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad skyed par byed pa'i yum gsang ba'i rdo rje 'dus pa thob ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa
6b6(rgyud 'bum): thams cad kyi yab dang lhan cig tu dga' ba'i bde ba rjes su byung ste 'khor dang bcas pa rnams bcom ldan 'das kyi spyan sngar lhags te/ rdo rje'i glu 'dis mngon par bstod nas zhu ba zhus pa/ sangs
6b7(rgyud 'bum): rgyas kun don khyod phyag 'tshal/ / rdo rje 'byung ba khyod la 'dud// thugs kyi rin chen mchog khyod 'dud// chos kyi blo gros khyod la 'dud// chos rnams kun mchog khyod la 'dud// sna tshogs
7a1(rgyud 'bum): dgongs pa khyod la 'dud/ / dam tshig mchog gi mchog khyod 'dud// rdo rje sems dpa' phyag 'tshal 'dud// grags pa chen po bdag cag ni// mgon po khyod la nubs/
7a2(rgyud 'bum): sangs rgyas thams cad skyed byed yum// dkyil 'khor gyi ni dkyil 'khor mchog/ de nas bcom ldan 'das rdo rje sems dpa' des de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rdo rje'i yum rnams la 'di
7a3(rgyud 'bum): skad ces bka' stsal to/ / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi yum rnams de skad ma smra zhig/ 'jig rten thams cad la khyab pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi rgyal po chen po 'di la ma 'ongs pa'i sems
7a4(rgyud 'bum): can rnams dad par mi 'gyur zhing / rang gi sems yongs su sun 'byin la/ des ma mthong ba'i chos la ma dad pas rang gi sems yang dag par sun phyung ste/ mnar med pa rnams su skyes nas
7a5(rgyud 'bum): bskal pa stong phrag mang por mnar med pa'i sdug bsngal rjes su 'byung bar 'gyur ro/ / de brgya lam na mnar med pa'i sdug bsngal las grol te/ mi rnams su skyes par gyur kyang rnam par 'gyur
7a6(rgyud 'bum): ba bzhin du 'gyur ro/ / brjed ngas pa rnams dang / blo gros chung ba rnams dang / khyi dang / bya rog dang / byi la dang / phag dang / stag dang / glang po che dang / seng ge'i nga ro 'dra ba dag tu 'gyur ro// de
7a7(rgyud 'bum): dang 'gre bar mi bya zhing blta bar mi bya'o/ / de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad bskyed pa'i yum de rnams kyis/ bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das ji ltar sems
7b1(rgyud 'bum): can de rnams kyi mnar med pa'i sdug bsngal zad par 'gyur/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ gang gis 'di'i ming bzung nas yongs su zad par 'gyur ro// bsod nams de'i rgyus
7b2(rgyud 'bum): de'i las kyi sgrib pa zad pa de bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub kyi skal ba can du 'gyur ro/ / de nas de dag yid dga' skyes nas yang / bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol
7b3(rgyud 'bum): to/ / bcom ldan 'das bstan du gsol/ bsod nams dang ye shes kyi tshogs kyi rgyus dkyil 'khor chen po'i rgyal po sems can thams cad la phan pa dang bde ba'i phyir/ gang ma
7b4(rgyud 'bum): 'ongs pa'i sems can rnams kyis dran pa tsam gyis sangs rgyas kyi byang chub thob par 'gyur ro/ / de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis kun tu bzang po chen po 'od 'phro ba gsal ba rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting
7b5(rgyud 'bum): nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs so/ / rang gi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje rnams las de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku'i dam pa 'di bka' stsal pa/ dkyil 'khor kun gyi yum
7b6(rgyud 'bum): gyur pa/ / stong nyid ye shes nyid du bshad// ci zhig nga yis bstan par bya// rtog pa thams cad rnam par spangs// sems can rnams la phan bzhed pa// gang zhig cung zad bstan par bya//
7b7(rgyud 'bum): de kun sgyu mas sgyu ma'o// 'gro ba sgyu ma lta bur shes// des na sgyu ma lta bu yis// sgyu ma lta bu'i dkyil 'khor bya// nam mkha'i khams kyis khyab pa yis// thams cad yum gyis yang dag
8a1(rgyud 'bum): 'khrugs/ / phyi rol yang ni brtag par bya// gsang ba'i dkyil 'khor lus rnams kyis// dben zhing dga' ba'i gnas su ni// yid kyis legs par 'dus byas pa/
8a2(rgyud 'bum): nam mkha' la ni thig gis gdab// thog mar de yis dam pas so// de nas rnal 'byor chen pos thig/ gsang ba'i yum gyi dkyil 'khor ro// su khyud dag gi rnam bdun du// kun nas yongs su
8a3(rgyud 'bum): bskor bar bya/ / dbus kyi cha ru dkyil 'khor ni// 'khor lo lta bur bri bar bya// kun nas brgyad gnyis mdzes pa ni// dkyil 'khor bzhi yi dbus su'o// 'khor lo'i lte ba'i dbus su ni// pad+ma
8a4(rgyud 'bum): ze 'bru ldan pa bri/ / mtshams dang mtshams su 'dab ma ni// ji lta ba bzhin bsnyems bcas pas// srang bu lnga yis yang dag 'khrugs// srad bu bzhi yis nye bar spras// sgo bzhi dang ni yang dag
8a5(rgyud 'bum): ldan/ / rtabapas seng ge dag gis brgyan// gdugs dang rgyal mtshan pa dan sogs// bla res steng du bres pa dang // rin chen rdo rje pad ldan sngon// dpag bsam shing gi lkug mas khyab// bum bzang
8a6(rgyud 'bum): rin chen ldan pa'i mchog/ rgyan 'phreng glang po ldan pa ni// phyi rol gnas te legs par bri// rtog dang mi rtog rnam spangs te// dkyil 'khor chen po'i dbus su ni// gsang ba rgyan gyi rdo rje bya// mnyam
8a7(rgyud 'bum): par gzhag cing spro ba yis/ / sems kyis bri ba nyid du bya// de nas lha mo zhal bzhim// shes rab pha rol phrin dge ba// phyag bzhi pa la spyan yangs ma// phyag gnyis kyis ni chos 'chad cing /
8b1(rgyud 'bum): zhi ba'i g.yas par rdo rje ste// g.yon pa pad+mas rnam par brgyan// dkar dang dmar po cher sngo ba// sngo bsangs rin chen mchog mdzes 'od// gtsug na rin chen gtsug tor che// gtsug rgyan cod pan dam
8b2(rgyud 'bum): pa can/ / skal ba chen po 'od ldan ma// rgyan rnams kun gyis rnam par klubs// gos kyis lto ni legs bsgribs pa// bzhin gyi dkyil 'khor 'dzum bcas shing // sna tshogs gos ni legs gyon pa// dbu
8b3(rgyud 'bum): ma'i zhal ras gser gyi 'od/ / zhabs gnyis dbus su 'khor lo ste// mdun na rin chen bdun gnas pa// pad+ma mchog ldan seng ge'i khri// zla ba rdo rje 'dzin pa'i gdan// nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor 'od 'phro ba// rgyab
8b4(rgyud 'bum): tu nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor ni/ / dpa' bo de yis bri bar bya// 'di yi mdun du bri bya ba// dpa' bo mtha' yas pa yi zhal// stong phrag du ma'i phyag ldan ma// mtshan nyid thams cad yang dag rdzogs// rgyan rnams
8b5(rgyud 'bum): kun gyis rnam par brgyan/ / phyag gi rdo rje pad+ma 'chang // sna tshogs phyag rgyas phyag gzhan dkrigs// btsug ldan dar gyi cod pan can// dbu rgyan pad+ma'i bzhin ras ma// zla ba'i dkyil 'khor dag la bzhum//

22a3(rgyud 'bum): los sgyur ba'i rim pa yis/ / 'khor lo rin chen bzang po'i lag/ rgyal ba rgyal ba'i sgra dge bas// gsang ba'i sbyor ba'i rnal 'byor gyis// lte ba ru ni dbang bskur ro// 'di bdag gtor can rin chen 'dzin//
22a4(rgyud 'bum): rdo rje rin chen 'dzin par 'gyur// dam tshig gi ni dam pa yis// sangs rgyas kun gyi don rgyas pa// 'bad pas de ring blangs pa yis// 'phongs pa'i dri ma 'phrog par byed// de nas dpa' bo 'chi med
22a5(rgyud 'bum): 'dzin/ / rin chen tshogs kyis mchod par bya// gzhan pa yi yang du ma ni// rgyal po dbang phyug dam pas so// de bzhin dbang bskur lnga po yis/ skabs med kyang ni bdag med 'gyur// gling bzhi'i
22a6(rgyud 'bum): dbang phyug dpal ldan yang / / gnod pa med par thob par 'gyur// gsang ba las kyang ches shin tu// gsang ba yis ni mna' bsgags te// de yi sgom dang sgrub pa'i thabs// slob ma la ni de
22a7(rgyud 'bum): nas bslab/ / gur kum dang ni tsan dan dang // dri dang mar me bzang po la// dam tshig gi ni gsal byas pa// lan gsum du ni 'thung du gzhug/ bu kye 'thung zhig gsang ba che// dam tshig shin tu
22b1(rgyud 'bum): 'da' ba dka'/ / gal te 'di las 'das gyur na// myur ba nyid du 'chi bar 'gyur// shi nas kyang ni dmyal sdug bsngal// rab mang ngu 'bod nyid du gnas// gal te mi ru skye 'dod pa 'am// nam
22b2(rgyud 'bum): zhig dngos grub thob 'dod na/ / de bzhin 'phongs pa'i sdug bsngal las// ring du nges par khyod kyis skyobs// 'di dag legs thos slob ma la// gsang ba'i sgrub thabs bshad par bya// ji ltar rgyal
22b3(rgyud 'bum): rigs bu mo ni/ / gzung nas gsal ba'i rnal 'byor bya// nyi ma bdun na nges par 'grub// rgyal po'i phun tshogs thob par 'gyur// shes rab pha rol phyin pa'i mchog/ dkyil 'khor sbyor bas bsam
22b4(rgyud 'bum): gtan bya/ / rgyal mo cho ga bzhin bzung ste// sgrub pa pos ni myur du 'grub// nyi ma gsum gyi rgyal po mchog/ gdon mi za bar thob par 'gyur// bram ze'i bu mo skal chen mo// nor chen la ni bsgrub par bya//
22b5(rgyud 'bum): rje rigs sna tshogs sbyor ba yis// mtshungs pa nyid du bsgrub par bya// de yis dngos grub mchog rnyed de// rgyal po 'jig rten gsum gyi rjed// dmangs mo dpa' bo'i sbyor ba yis// bsgrubs na sngags kyi
22b6(rgyud 'bum): dngos grub 'gyur/ / gnod sbyin rgyal mchog grub pa dang // gnod sbyin rnams kyi dbang phyug mchog/ dman pa'i sems su bshad pa dang // mchog gis mchog ni chen po dang // bar mas bar ma'i dngos
22b7(rgyud 'bum): grub ni/ / skye ba 'di la thob par 'gyur// de nas las rnams bslab par bya// zhi ba dang ni rgyas pa'i las// de bzhin dbang dang mngon spyod dang // gzhan pa yi yang sna tshogs ni// sems can rnams la/
23a1(rgyud 'bum): dga' ba'o// shes rab pha rol phyin dge ma// dkyil 'khor sbyor bas bsgom par bya// kun dkar po zla ba 'dra// 'od zer dkar pos mdzes pa mo// skye bo nad pa 'a
23a2(rgyud 'bum): ka ma/ / de yi lus la gzhug par bya// de nas de ni stobs ldan 'gyur// brgyad gnyis pa yi lang tshor ldan// nad rnams kun las rnam par grol// rga dang 'chi ba rnam par spangs// bstan bcos
23a3(rgyud 'bum): kun gyi don rig cing / / shes rab dran pa mchog dang ldan// de bzhin rang 'gyur rnal 'byor pa// nam mkha' la ni yang dag bsgom// mdzes pa'i rin chen sna tshogs pa'i// thams cad du ni char 'bab pa//
23a4(rgyud 'bum): 'di yis 'phongs pa rnam par sel// 'phongs pa rnams la rab tu brtag/ mthe bong gi ni tshad tsam pa'i// nor rgyun ma yi rnam pa bya// lha mo la ni mnyam par gzhag/ de yi mdun du gsang sngags bzlas//
23a5(rgyud 'bum): ji srid 'bum phrag kho na ste// de nas dngos grub bsgrub par bya// zla ba gang ba'am bcu bzhi 'am// brgyad pa'am gzas bzung nyin bar la// mchod pa chen po byas nas su// mkhas pas mtshan mo thog/
23a6(rgyud 'bum): thag bzlas// de nas dga' bas gzugs brnyan de// gdon mi za bar 'bar bar 'gyur// de nas bzung ste mdor bsdu na// mi yi 'khor los sgyur bar 'gyur// bzlas pas mtshan ma bzang byung na//
23a7(rgyud 'bum): rnal 'byor pa ni nor chen 'gyur// bar mas gling ni thob par 'gyur// tha ma yis ni khor yug go// thams cad du ni bzlas tsam gyis// longs spyod zad par 'gyur ma yin// rgyal po thams cad dbang
23b1(rgyud 'bum): 'gyur zhing / / bud med thams cad dga' bar 'gyur// snying khar rnal 'byor byas nas su// nor bu lag par bcangs nas ni// nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor la gnas bsgom// myur du rin chen rgyal por
23b2(rgyud 'bum): 'gyur/ / phyag rgya 'di ni byas gyur pas// rtag tu sgom pas bsgom par bya// ji ltar 'dod pa'i grub rnyed de// rdo rje 'dzin pa ji bzhin no// zhes bcom ldan 'das rdo rje sems dpas bka' stsal te//
23b3(rgyud 'bum): de nas sbyor ba ji bzhin du// yum de rnams ni legs byon nas// las kyi dkyil 'khor legs gnas pa// ston pa la ni zhu ba zhus// gang du rgyal ba kun bzhugs nas// bla na med pa'i don mdzad pa//
23b4(rgyud 'bum): sems can kun la bde slad du// myur du las ni 'grub pa legs// de nas bcom ldan 'das las thams cad kyi dam pa'i dpal zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa
23b5(rgyud 'bum): thams cad kyi yum gyi dam tshig gi dam pa de rnams la las kyi dkyil 'khor bka' stsal pa/ rlung gi dkyil 'khor bri bar bya// de yi dbus su gru gsum pa// de yi steng du lha mo gzhag/ 'bar ba'i me dang
23b6(rgyud 'bum): mtshungs pa la/ / zhal bzhi ma la cher 'jigs pa// mche ba rab tu gtsigs pa mo// thod pa'i 'breng ba'i cod pan can// rdo rje lcags kyu thod pa dang // zhags pa g.yas dang g.yon par 'dzin//
23b7(rgyud 'bum): pags pa chen po gos su gyon// khro mo mig 'bras rab phyung ba// mche bas mchu mnan zhal chen mo// de yi mdun du bri bya ba// mtha' ma'i zhal ni mdor bsdus pa// sna tshogs gtum dang drag pa'i
24a1(rgyud 'bum): zhal/ / du ma'i phyag gis yang dka' khrugs// zhags pa lcags kyu thod sogs dang // rdo rje can gyi sog le 'dzin// thod pas lus la bres gyur cing // cod pan
24a2(rgyud 'bum): chen pos 'jigs byed mo/ / gshini rje dpa' bos bri bya ba// mtha' gdong dam pa yi ni mchog/ sngon po 'bar ba'i rang bzhin khros// mgo bo'i 'phreng bas rnam par brgyan// thod pa'i 'phreng ba'i
24a3(rgyud 'bum): cod pan can/ / stag gi pags pa'i sham thabs can// ral gri rin chen thod pa dang // rin chen dbyug gu 'dzin pa'i mchog/ de nas lha mo legs bri ba// pad+ma'i zhal ma 'jigs chen po// dmar mo phyag na
24a4(rgyud 'bum): nyizla 'dzin/ / bskal pa'i me dang mtshungs pa mo// g.yon pa ru ni khro mo che// ma sprom ma ni ska rags mgul// las kyi rdo rje dri ldan mchog/ mche ba rnam par gtsigs pa'i zhal// gtsug na thod pa 'jigs su rung //
24a5(rgyud 'bum): rab gtum stobs dang gsal ba mo// 'byor ldan cho ga rig pas bris// phyi rol tu ni legs bri ba// khro bcas 'jigs pa dang bcas pa// ral pa'i thor tsugs chen po can// khrag gis gang ba'i thod pa dang //
24a6(rgyud 'bum): phyag rgya bzang pos phyag mtshan pa'o// de yi phyi ru lha rnams ni// snyim pa rab sbyar yi dam pa// thams cad du ni yongs su gzhag/ 'jig rten skyong ba gzhag par bya// sgo rnams dag ni thams cad du// sgo skyong ba
24a7(rgyud 'bum): yang de bzhin du/ / de nas gtor ma'i cho ga ni// sha bcas btung ba ro dang ldan// de nas go cha bcings gyur pas// thod pa'i cod pan chen po dang // khrag gam chang gis bkang ba 'am// thod pa ldan pas 'jig par
24b1(rgyud 'bum): bya/ / thams cad 'grub pa'i ma mo rnams// 'di yis spyan ni drang bar bya// dkon mchog gsum la gnod byed pa'i// gsad pa'i don dum mo rnams// de ring nyid du dkyil 'khor 'dir// 'jigs
24b2(rgyud 'bum): chen ma rnams thams cad gshegs/ / 'jigs pa'i sgra dang cher gtum dang // kha nas 'od zer stong phrag ni// mthong ba dang ni thos pa na// mtshan mar yang ni shes par bya// de nas de yis arga sbyin//
24b3(rgyud 'bum): bder ba zhes shig 'jigs mdzadas// gdug pa chen mo gsol bar mdzod// gdug gtus 'jigs par byed pa yis// de nas bdag la dbang bskur te// thod par gnas pa'i ro yis ni// srang tsam gyi nig rdos
24b4(rgyud 'bum): nas/ / ma mo thams cad bsgrub par bya// de nas mngon spyod las rnams kun// dam tshig bsrung ba yis ni bya// dkon mchog gsum la gnod byed dang // bla ma rnams la 'khyal smra ba// rtag tu gsod par
24b5(rgyud 'bum): lha mo rnams/ / bgyid par bdag ni rjes su zung // de nas cho ga de nyid kyis// slob ma'i dam pa gzhug par bya// khro bo'i lha la bskul nas su// me tog dmar po dor bar bya// bdag gi me tog dam pa
24b6(rgyud 'bum): 'di/ / ci bde bar ni bzhes su gsol// bdug pa 'di ni bzung nas su// gsol byed 'di ni gsol bar mdzod// lha mo gang la lhung gyur pa// de yis de la mchog gsol lo// de nas dbang bskur
24b7(rgyud 'bum): byin nas su/ / dkyil 'khor gyi ni mdun gzhag ste// thod pa ru ni gnas pa yis// khrag gis dbang ni bskur bar bya// de nas sgo ru bos nas su// dam tshig 'bad pas 'dzin du gzhug/ rab tu
25a1(rgyud 'bum): gdug pa'i snying gi khrag/ bzang po 'di ni 'thung zhig bu// zo zhig zo zhig sha chen po// btung ba 'jigs pa chen po 'thung // gzhan du na ni 'chi 'gyur te// mkha' 'gro
25a2(rgyud 'bum): ma dang gza' rnams dang / / gnod sbyin srin po gtum po yis// ring por mi thogs rab tu za// de nas mngon spyod las rnams ni// stong phrag dag ni bslab par bya// de yi sbyor ba'i rnal 'byor gyis//
25a3(rgyud 'bum): rang nyid khro bor bzung gyur nas// gnod byed thams cad gsad par bya// dgra rnams thams cad bza' bar bya// gdug pa thams cad bca' bar bya// srin po thams cad gzhom par bya// mtha' yas
25a4(rgyud 'bum): zhal ma'i sbyor ba yis/ / gsad dang gzung ba de yis bya// zhal bzhi ma yi sbyor ba yis// thams cad 'gugs pa'i dam pa yin// mkha' gdong ma yis thams cad du// rin po che yi tshogs 'byung ngo //
25a5(rgyud 'bum): pad+ma'i zhal gyi sbyor ba yis// chang gi dam pa btung bar bya// ma sprom ma yi sbyor ba yis// sha ni 'gugs pa'i mchog yin no// nam mkhas rengs pa chen po ste// dmag dpung 'byor pa'i dam pa'o//
25a6(rgyud 'bum): rmugs dang rmongs pa thams cad du// dpyad pa ru ni mi bya'o// sngar bshad pa yi las rnams dang // ma bshad pa la ci 'dod pa// bzlas pa tsam gyis kun bya ste// thams cad du ni the tsom med// dur
25a7(rgyud 'bum): khrod kyi ni thal ba la/ / dgra bo'i gzugs ni 'bad pas bya// ming dang spel bar byas nas su// ma mo'i ral gris gtub par bya// de nas nyi ma bdun na ni// rlag par 'gyur bar gdon mi za// gang lus
25b1(rgyud 'bum): ji ltar bcad gyur pa/ / de dang de yi yan lag 'chad// zhal bzhi ma yi sbyor ba yis// sngags pa mnyam par gzhag pas bcad// de yi mgrin par zhags pa ni// mkhas pas spros te bcing bar
25b2(rgyud 'bum): bya/ / lcags kyus snying khar phug nas su// rlung gis bskyod de drang bar bya// de nas de yi ming bskul nas// de ni shes rab ldan pas dgug/ dman dang mchog gi dbye ba yis// 'di yi 'bras bu nga
25b3(rgyud 'bum): yis bshad/ / mdor bsdus pas ni shes par bya// sngags pa'i rgyal po sbyor ba yis// shes so// de nas bcom ldan 'das ma de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad ni/ de yis dngos grub gsol mi

25b6(rgyud 'bum): bus yab gyur bsgrubs na ni/ / nyi ma bdun na rab tu 'grub// sangs rgyas kun gyi yab ston pa// kun mkhyen ye shes spyod yul te// drag po kun dang bde chen po// ye shes kun gyi mchog gi mchog

26a1(rgyud 'bum): par bya/ / shes rab kyi ni las dbye bas// gzugs dang dbyibs nyid dag gis so// phyag rgya dang ni phyag rgya'i lan// de bzhin dkyil 'khor dam tshig dang // bza' ba dang ni nyer spyod

28a1(rgyud 'bum): 'gyur/ / rig pa 'di yis de yis ni// las rnams thams cad byed pa dang // dbang dang dgug dang dbye ba dang // tshim dang 'phrog dang 'bras chen po// zhi bas zhi ba zhes su

28a3(rgyud 'bum): dag ldan/ / sor mo zhags pas dkri bar bya// thams cad du ni drag po dgug/ drag po drag po'i go 'phang gnas// 'di yi cho ga ldan pa yis// las kyi tshogs kyi mchog kun bya// sems la rnal
